***тюлень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюлень.html>тюле́нь</a> (22220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sami_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sami languages">Sami</a></span> language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Sami" class="extiw" title="w:Northern Sami">Northern Sami</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="se">dealljá</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюлень.html>тюле́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjulénʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюлень.html>тюле́ня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюлень.html>тюле́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюлень.html>тюле́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>seal (pinniped)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A clumsy person, an oaf</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">turban</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">tülbent</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">muslin; cheesecloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">دلبند</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolband</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***тюрьма.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьма́</a> (1240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Traditionally derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">turma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">turm</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">turn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">*torn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">turrem</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="la">turrim</i>, accusative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">turris</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tower</i>. But more likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Turkic language">Proto-Turkic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="trk-pro">*türmä</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">төрмә</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">törmä</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kyrgyz_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kyrgyz language">Kyrgyz</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ky">түрмө</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ky-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">türmö</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьма́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjurʹmá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьмы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тю́рьмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тю́рем</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>prison, jail</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тюремник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tjuremnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***тюфяк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфя́к</a> (18114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tt">tüšäk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mattress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; dialectally <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тюша́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjušák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Modern form probably influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфя́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjufják</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">early type of firearm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see below).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфя́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjufják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфяка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфяко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mattress; a sack filled with something soft (e.g. hay) to be used as a mattress</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wimp, weakling, wuss, coward</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mattress <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">retaining wall of brushwood, concrete, etc. to protect the river bed and banks of bridges and dams from erosion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Siberia<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sandpiper</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mattress</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрац.html>матра́ц</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">matrác</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрас.html>матра́с</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">matrás</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тюфякъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjufjakŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Turkic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Turkic">Old Turkic</a></span> <i class="Orkh mention" lang="otk">tüfäk</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="otk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tüfäk</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tube, gun, crossbow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфя́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjufják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфяка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюфяк.html>тюфяко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> early type of firearm</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тявкать.html>тя́вкать</a> (26015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тявкать.html>тя́вкать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjávkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тявкнуть.html>тя́вкнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to yap, to yelp <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a small dog, to bark in a non-growly manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">disparagingly</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to object, to protest aloud, to talk back, to complain</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́га</a> (7279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjaga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tęgъ</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tęga</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>draft/draught, pull, draw</li>
<li>traction, pulling, hauling</li>
<li>thrust</li>
<li>pull rod, connecting rod</li>
<li>stay, brace</li>
<li>laboratory hood</li>
<li>bent, desire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">hunting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> roding, flight of woodcock in mating season</li></ol>

***тягать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тягать.html>тяга́ть</a> (27759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tędzati</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tęgati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягать.html>тяга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjagátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потяга́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull, to drag</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry around (especially something heavy)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягость.html>тя́гость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjágostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягостный.html>тя́гостный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjágostnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>burdensome, onerous</li>
<li>painful, distressing

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тягостный.html>тя́гостное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зрелище.html>зре́лище</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tjágostnoje</b> zrélišče</i> ― <span class="e-translation">distressing/painful sight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тягостный.html>тя́гостное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчание.html>молча́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tjágostnoje</b> molčánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">oppressive silence</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тягота</a> (16886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тя́гота</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjágota</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тя́готы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тя́готы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тя́гот</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тя́гота</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjágota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготеть.html>тяготе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjagotétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be strongly attracted, to have a propensity/bent, to be drawn, to be strongly attached</li>
<li>to hang <i>(over)</i>, to weigh <i>(upon)</i>, to threaten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготеть.html>тяготе́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обвинение.html>обвине́ние</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nad nim <b>tjagotéjet</b> strášnoje obvinénije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he lies under a terrible accusation; a terrible accusation hangs over him</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяготеющий.html>тяготе́ющий</a> (19348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготеющий.html>тяготе́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjagotéjuščij</span>)
</p>

***тяготить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́ть</a> (15847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягота.html>тя́гота</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjágota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjagotítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be a burden <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto menjá ne <b>tjagotít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't find it burdensome</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to oppress
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá <b>tjagotít</b> jevó drúžba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his friendship irks me; I find his friendship burdensome/irksome</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молчание.html>молча́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начинать.html>начина́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">molčánije načinálo <b>tjagotítʹ</b> nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">our silence was becoming oppressive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совесть.html>со́весть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto <b>tjagotít</b> jevó sóvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it lies heavy on his conscience</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночество.html>одино́чество</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяготить.html>тяготи́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">odinóčestvo jevó <b>tjagotít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his loneliness oppresses/depresses him</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тягучий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тягучий.html>тягу́чий</a> (10642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тягучий.html>тягу́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjagúčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>viscous, viscid, syrupy, malleable, ductile</li>
<li><i>(song etc)</i> slow, leisured, leisurely</li></ol>

***тяжелеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелеть.html>тяжеле́ть</a> (24806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjažólyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелеть.html>тяжеле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjaželétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to grow heavy, to increase in weight</li>
<li>to put on weight, to grow sluggish</li>
<li><i>(eyes, eyelids)</i> to become heavy with sleep</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжело́</a> (1270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжело́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjaželó</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-тяжело́" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тяжеле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-тяжело́" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелеть.html>тяжеле́й</a></b>)
